                       Top Colleges in India 2026
                    </h1><div class="userDetail"><div class="userImg"><a href="/author/amit-singh/"><img src="https://static.collegedekho.com/static-v3/images/college_listing/userIcon.0a54c70dabfb.svg" width="24" height="24" alt="Amit Singh"><img class="verificationTick" src="https://static.collegedekho.com/static-v3/images/college_listing/verifiedTick.197f53ec3d9f.svg" width="19" height="19" alt="Verified Author"></a></div><div class="writerInfo"><div class="writerName">Written By 
                                        <a href="/author/amit-singh/" target="_blank"> Amit Singh - Content Writer</a></div><div class="timeAndDate">Updated on - Feb 11, 2026 11:45 PM IST</div></div></div><div class="content ReadMore " id="div-content"><p>India has developed a significant number of higher education institutions over time to meet the demand of the expanding youth population by providing quality education, so we have prepared a list of top colleges in India 2026. These colleges have established themselves not only nationally but also internationally. India has long been a centre for education worldwide. Students from over the world view Indian colleges as the best places to learn in large part due to a variety of factors including a rich, multifaceted culture, breakthroughs in technology, a broad selection of courses, well-equipped labs, and a low cost of living.</p><p>India has a vast education system with over 43,000 colleges and 1,100+ universities offering courses in a number of disciplines like engineering, medical, management, law and arts. Out of these, approximately 65.3% are private un-aided, 13.2% are private aided, and 21.5% are government colleges. Admissions to these colleges are based on various exams like CUET, JEE, CLAT, CAT, XAT, MAT, NEET, and other state and college specific exams. Some colleges also offer direct admission based on class 12th marks. The cutoffs for government colleges are usually high because of their affordability, and better reputation. Although some private colleges like BITS Pilani, IIIT Hyderabad, and others are as good as government colleges in terms of reputation.  </p><p>IITs and IIMs are renowned as centres of excellence. Numerous liberal arts colleges have recently been established in India in an effort to advance the multidisciplinary system of education. It not only offers students a substitute for Ivy League institutions but also demonstrates the bright future of liberal arts education in India. The most popular among these are Management (7893), Engineering (6705), Information Technology (6142), Commerce &amp; Banking (4959), Hotel Management (1630), and Design (1505). For admissions, 1529 colleges accept CMAT, 710 accept CAT, 548 consider JEE Mains, 489 accept MAT, 326 take TNEA, and 320 recognize XAT. Hostel facilities are available in 5344 colleges for boys and 2202 for girls. This article lists top colleges in India based on multiple factors like placement, cutoff, fees, courses and others.</p><div class="scrollTable"><table><thead><tr><th style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:283px;"><p><strong>Particulars</strong></p><p></p><p></p></th><th style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:331px;"><p><strong>Statistics</strong></p><p></p><p></p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:283px;"><p>Recognitions and Affiliations </p><p></p></td><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:331px;"><ul><li>Recognition: UGC</li><li>Accreditation: NAAC</li><li>Approval: AICTE</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:283px;">Top Specializations</td><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:331px;"><ul><li>Engineering</li><li>Architecture</li><li>Arts</li><li>Commerce</li><li>Management</li><li>Medical and more</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:283px;"><p>Entrance Exam Accepted                                                                                   </p><p></p></td><td style="padding:7px;vertical-align:top;width:331px;"><ul><li>CUET - UG</li><li>CUET - PG</li><li>IIT JAM</li><li>JEE Main </li><li>NEET - UG &amp; PG and more               </li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2><img loading="lazy" src="https://media.collegedekho.com/media/cms/ck5/India.png"/>Top 25 Colleges in India Based on NIRF 2025</h2><p>The National Institutional Ranking Framework (NIRF) is India’s official annual ranking system for higher education institutions. It ranks universities, colleges, and professional schools across 11+ categories (including engineering, management, and medical) based on five main parameters: teaching, research, graduation outcomes, outreach, and perception. Here are the top 25 colleges that were ranked by NIRF and the popular courses they offer.</p><div class="scrollTable"><table><thead><tr><th style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;"><p style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">5–7 Lakhs</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p><br/></p><h2><strong>Admission Process through CUET </strong></h2><p>The Common University Entrance Examination (CUET) is the most popular exam for admission to undergraduate courses in some prominent universities like University of Delhi, Jamia Millia Islamia, Guru Gobind Singh Indraprastha University. The admission process through CUET is as follows.</p><ul><li>Step-1 Register for CUET and Select Subjects - Candidates must first register for CUET on the official NTA portal. While filling the application form, students should carefully choose subjects according to the course-wise subject mapping prescribed by their preferred universities. Selecting incorrect subjects can lead to rejection during counselling, so this step is crucial.</li><li>Step-2 Appear for the CUET Exam - CUET is conducted in computer-based mode (CBT) at designated exam centres. The exam tests candidates on selected domain subjects, language papers, and/or the General Test, depending on the course requirements.</li><li>Step-3 Check Results and Download Scorecard - After the exam, NTA releases CUET results online. Candidates must download and save their CUET scorecard, which is mandatory for applying to participating universities.</li><li>Step-4 Apply to Universities Using CUET Scores - CUET scores do not automatically guarantee admission. Candidates must separately apply on the admission portals of universities they are interested in, such as Delhi University or Jamia Millia Islamia, using their CUET application number and scores.</li><li>Step-5 Merit Lists and Counselling - Universities prepare course-wise merit lists based on CUET scores, category, and eligibility criteria. Shortlisted candidates are invited to participate in online or offline counselling rounds conducted by the respective universities.</li><li>Step-6 Seat Allotment and Admission Confirmation - Based on merit rank and preferences, seats are allotted to candidates. Students must then verify documents, pay the admission fee, and confirm their seat within the specified deadline to secure admission.</li></ul><p>The table below outlines the CUET schedule 2026 highlighting the important dates and details</p><div class="scrollTable"><table><thead><tr><th style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-align:center;"><strong>Event</strong></p></th><th style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-align:center;"><strong>Date</strong></p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Registration Start</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">January 2026                                                                                                                                                </td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Registration Last Date</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">February 04, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Last Date to Pay Application Fee                                                                                                             </td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">February 07, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Application Correction Window</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">February 09 - February 11, 2026                                                                                                                  </td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Admit Card Release</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">May 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Exam Dates</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">May 11 - May 31, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Result Declaration</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">June 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">CUET Counselling Process</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">June - July 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Exam Mode</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Computer Based Test (CBT)</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Official Website</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">cuet.nta.nic.in</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2><strong>Admission Process through JEE Mains </strong></h2><p>The Joint Entrance Examination (JEE) Mains is a crucial examination for engineering students. Most colleges in Delhi accept it for admission. Admission to engineering colleges is based on JoSAA counselling. Here is a step by step process explaining the same.</p><ul><li>Step-1 Register for JEE Main - Candidates must first register for JEE Main on the official NTA portal. While filling out the application form, students need to enter personal and academic details, choose the exam session, select preferred exam cities, and upload the required documents. Timely and accurate form submission is essential to avoid rejection.</li><li>Step-2 Appear for the JEE Main Exam - JEE Main is conducted in computer-based mode (CBT) at designated exam centres. Paper 1 is conducted for BE/BTech, while Paper 2A and 2B are for BArch and BPlan. The exam tests candidates on Physics, Chemistry, and Mathematics.</li><li>Step-3 Check Results and Download Scorecard - After the exam, NTA releases the JEE Main results online. Candidates must download and save their JEE Main scorecard, which contains percentile scores and All India Rank (AIR) required for counselling and admissions.</li><li>Step-4 Apply for Counselling Using JEE Main Scores - JEE Main scores do not automatically ensure admission. Candidates must apply through counselling processes such as JoSAA counselling for NITs, IIITs, and GFTIs. For engineering colleges in Delhi like DTU, NSUT, and IIIT Delhi, admissions are conducted through JAC Delhi counselling based on JEE Main ranks.</li><li>Step-5 Counselling and Seat Allotment - Counselling authorities prepare merit lists based on JEE Main rank, category, and preferences. Through JoSAA or JAC Delhi, candidates are allotted seats in multiple rounds depending on availability and choices filled.</li><li>Step-6 Admission Confirmation and Reporting - Once a seat is allotted, candidates must verify documents, pay the admission fee, and confirm the seat within the given deadline. Final admission is confirmed after reporting to the allotted institute or completing online verification.</li></ul><p>The following table summarises the JEE Mains examination schedule for 2026. Candidates can go through the schedule and prepare accordingly.</p><div class="scrollTable"><table><thead><tr><th style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-align:center;"><strong>Event</strong></p></th><th style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-align:center;"><strong>Date / Details</strong></p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Notification Release</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">October 31, 2025</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Application Start - Session 1</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">October 31, 2025</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Application Last Date - Session 1                                                                                                                             </td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">November 27, 2025</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">City Intimation Slip - Session 1</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">January 08, 2026                                                                                                                          </td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Exam Dates - Paper 1 (BE/BTech)</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">January 21, 22, 23, 24, 28, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Exam Date - Paper 2A &amp; 2B (BArch / BPlan)</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">January 29, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Application Start - Session 2</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">January 31, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Application Last Date - Session 2</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">February 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Exam Dates - Session 2</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">April 02 to April 09, 2026</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Courses Offered</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">BE/BTech, BArch, BPlan</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Exam Mode</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Computer Based Test (CBT)</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Conducting Authority</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">National Testing Agency</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">Official Website</td><td style="padding:5pt;vertical-align:top;">jeemain.nta.ac.in</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p><br/><br/><br/></p><h2><strong>Best Colleges in India - Region Wise 2026</strong></h2><p>When it comes to the availability of higher education facilities, both the south and the north of India are home to a large number of reputable colleges that provide a wide range of programmes in practically every field. FAQs</strong></h2><p><strong>Ques. What are some of the top colleges in India?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> Some of the top colleges in India 2025 are Miranda House, Hindu College, Presidency College, Loyola College, Lady Shri Ram College for Women. These colleges are ranked as per the latest NIRF ranking 2025.</p><p><strong>Ques. How many colleges are there in the state of Uttarakhand?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> There are approximately 121 colleges present in the state of Uttarakhand. Nearly 3 constituent and 118 affiliated colleges are there in the state of Uttarakhand.</p><p><strong>Ques. What factors are considered for carrying out the NIRF ranking?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> Five factors are taken into consideration by the Ministry of Education while determining the NIRF rankings: Teacher, Learning &amp; Resource (TLR), Research, Professional Practice &amp; Collaborative Performance (RPC), Graduation Outcome (GO), Outreach and Inclusivity (OI), Perception (PR).</p><p><strong>Ques. As per the placement records 2026, what are the top colleges in India?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> As per the placement records 2025, some of the top colleges in India are IIT Delhi, IIT Madras, IIT Bombay, IIT Kharagpur and more. Some of the major recruiting participants at these colleges are Amazon, Google, Microsoft, Myntra, Flipkart, Cognizant, Havells, Infosys and more.</p><p><strong>Ques. What are some of the top commerce colleges in India?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> The top commerce colleges in India are Shri Ram College of Commerce, Lady Shri Ram College for Women, Loyola College, St. Xaviers' College, Symbiosis College of Arts and Commerce and Narsee Monjee College of Commerce and Economics.</p><p><strong>Ques. What are the possible career options after pursuing BA literature courses in India?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> Job profiles like content writer, HR executive, copywriter, scriptwriter, teacher, and journalist are some of the options that are available for literature graduates from reputed colleges in India.</p><p><strong>Ques. Why are QS World University Rankings important?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans. </strong>The top universities in the world are ranked each year in 51 distinct and five composite sectors by Quacquarelli Symonds Limited's QS World University Rankings. This ranking helps us to identify the best colleges and universities in the country depending on various factors such as placement, entrance exam, admission process and more.</p><p><strong>Ques. What are the top BA Hons programmes offered at the University of Delhi?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> The most popular BA Hons programmes at the University of Delhi include BA Hons in English, BA Hons in Psychology, BA Hons in Economics, BA Hons in Political Science, and BA Hons in History.</p><p><strong>Ques. What are some of India's most well-known university entrance exams?</strong></p><p><strong>Ans.</strong> CUET - UG &amp; PG, TISSNET, Aligarh Muslim University Entrance Test, Calcutta University Entrance Exam, IIT JAM, and CPGET are a few of the top entrance exams that are considered for admission to various courses in India.</p><p><strong>Ques. What are some of the top management colleges in India?</strong></p><p>Ans. Some of the topmost management colleges in India are IIM Ahmedabad, IIM Bangalore, IIM Kolkata, IIT Delhi, and IIM Lucknow. Management courses are offered in a variety of specialisations to interested candidates such as human resources, aviation, hotel management and more.</p><p>​</p><p></p></div><a href="#" id="top-content-a-read-more" class="read-more" data-id="div-content" data-more="ReadLess" data-less="ReadMore">Read More

window.requestIdleCallback = window.requestIdleCallback || function(handler) {
  let startTime = Date.now();

  return setTimeout(function() {
    handler({
      didTimeout: false,
      timeRemaining: function() {
        return Math.max(0, 50.0 - (Date.now() - startTime));
      }
    });
  }, 1);
}

loadScript = function(src, scriptID) {
    var existingScript = document.getElementById(scriptID);
    if(existingScript){
        return;
    }

    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
        let script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = src;
        script.defer = true;
        script.id=scriptID;
        script.onload = () => resolve(script);
        script.onerror = () => reject(new Error(`Script load error for ${src}`));
        document.head.append(script);

  });
}

loadStyle = function(src,styleID)
{
            var existingStyle = document.getElementById(styleID);
            if(existingStyle){
                return;
            }

            return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                var style = document.createElement('link');
                style.href = src;
                style.type = 'text/css';
                style.rel = 'stylesheet';
                style.onload = () => resolve(style);
                style.onerror = () => reject(new Error(`style load error for ${src}`));
                document.head.append(style);
            });
};

get_login_modal = function (button, qna_login,callBack)
{
    if(qna_login == true || button.parentNode.getAttribute('id')=="login")
    {
        url = "/accounts/login/?next="+"/colleges-in-india/"
        console.log(url)
    }
    else
    {
        url = "/accounts/signup/?next="+"/colleges-in-india/"
    }
    $.ajax({
        url:url,
        type:"GET",
        data:{},

        success:function(data)
        {
            $('body').addClass('bodyScroll');
            $('#popup-body').html(data)
            if (!($(window).width() <= 767)){
                //var popupHeight = ($('.loginPage .wrapper').height())/2; 
                //$('.loginPage .wrapper').css({"margin-top":'-' + popupHeight +'px'});
            }
            $('.loginPage .close').click(function(){
                $('.loginPage').fadeOut(400);
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $(".loginPage .wrapper").removeAttr('style');
                }, 1000);
                $('.loginPage').remove();
                if(downloadTimer)
                {
                    clearInterval(downloadTimer);
                }

            });

            if (url.indexOf('login') >= 0) 
            {
              $('#signUp').hide();
              $('#otpVerification1').show();
            } else {
              $('#signUp').show();
              $('#otpVerification1').hide();
            }
            if(typeof(callBack) === 'function')
            {
                callBack();
            }
        },
        error:function()
        {
        }
    });
}

ajax_submit_login = function(e)
{

    $("#loader").show()
    e.preventDefault();
    $.ajax(
    {
        url:"/accounts/login/",
        type:"POST",
        data:$("#login-form").serialize(),
        success:function(response)
        {
                if(response.token){
                    updateLocalStorage(response.token)
                }

                var currentUrl = location.href
                $("#loader").hide()
                document.getElementById("loader").style.display = "none";
                if(response.location && reloadOnLogin){
                    // Call Website Login Event
                    var userIdentifier = response?.token?.user?.user_identifier
                    trackWebsiteLogin(response.user_id, userIdentifier)
                    if(currentUrl.includes("?next=")){

                        window.location.href = response.location    
                        window.location.reload(true);
                    }
                    else{
                        location.href = "/my-dashboard"
                    }
                }
                else if (response.location && !reloadOnLogin){
                    $('.loginPage').fadeOut(400);
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $(".loginPage .wrapper").removeAttr('style');
                    }, 1000);
                    $('.loginPage').remove();
                    $('body').removeClass("bodyScroll");
                    isLoggedIn = 1
                    $('#is-logged-in').val(1);

                    //Call Website Login Event
                    var userIdentifier = response?.token?.user?.user_identifier
                    trackWebsiteLogin(response.user_id, userIdentifier)
                }
                else if(response.html && response.form_errors){
                    $('body').append(response.html);
                }
             
        },
        error:function(error)
        {
            $("#loader").hide()
            $(".error").html('');
            var err = JSON.parse(error.responseText)
            //Object.keys(err['form_errors']).forEach(function(e){
            //    $("#login-form > ul > li.last-li").before("<li class='error'>"+(err['form_errors'][e][0])+"</li>")});


            Object.keys(err['form_errors']).forEach(function(e){
                $("#login-form "+"."+e).after("<p class='error'>"+err['form_errors'][e]+"</p>");
                })
                if(err.form_errors['__all__'] != undefined){
                $("#signIn .password").after('<p class="error">'+err.form_errors['__all__']+'</p>');
        }


        }
    });
}

(function() {
    window.AnalyticsLoader = {
        services: {},
        loadedServices: new Set(),
        
        register: function(serviceName) {
            this.services[serviceName] = false;
        },
        
        markLoaded: function(serviceName) {
            this.services[serviceName] = true;
            this.loadedServices.add(serviceName);
            this.checkAllLoaded();
        },
        
        checkAllLoaded: function() {
            const allLoaded = Object.keys(this.services).every(
                service => this.services[service] === true
            );
            
            if (allLoaded && Object.keys(this.services).length > 0) {
                this.onAllServicesLoaded();
            }
        },
        
        onAllServicesLoaded: function() {
            console.log('All analytics services loaded:', Array.from(this.loadedServices));
            
            if (typeof trackOnLoadEvents === 'function') {
                trackOnLoadEvents();
            }
        }
    };
})();

function webEngageTrack() {
    var user_id;
    if ("False" == 'False') {
        user_id = localStorage.getItem("user_id");
    } else {
        user_id = None;
    }
    
    if (user_id && webengage.state.getForever() && 
        webengage.state.getForever().cuid != user_id) {
        webengage.user.logout();
        webengage.user.login(user_id);
    }
    window.AnalyticsLoader.markLoaded('webengage');
}

function loadCleverTap() {
    window?.AnalyticsLoader.register('clevertap');

    (function () {
        var wzrk = document.createElement('script');
        wzrk.type = 'text/javascript';
        wzrk.async = true;
        wzrk.src = ('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://d2r1yp2w7bby2u.cloudfront.net' : 'http://static.clevertap.com') + '/js/clevertap.min.js';
        wzrk.onload = function () {
            window.AnalyticsLoader.markLoaded('clevertap');
            let userIdentifier = localStorage.getItem("user_identifier");
            userIdentifier && clevertap.onUserLogin.push({"Site": {"Identity": userIdentifier}});
        };
        var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        s.parentNode.insertBefore(wzrk, s);
    })();
}

function loadMetaPixelScript(){
    if (window.AnalyticsLoader.services?.fbPixel) return;
    window.AnalyticsLoader.register('fbPixel');

    if (!window.fbq) {
        !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s){

            n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
            if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;
            n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
            n.queue=[];

            s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
            s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s);
        }(window, document,'script','https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');
    }
    fbq('init', '204674529973597');
    fbq('init', '806395515092654');
    fbq('track', 'PageView');

    window.AnalyticsLoader.markLoaded('fbPixel');
}

                   if($('#div1').hasClass('selected')) {
                        $('#div1').removeClass('selected')
                        $('#div2').addClass('selected')
                    }
            });
        }


        function removeFilter(that) {
            $(".loading_div").css({"display": "block"});
            var tags = []
            uri = $(that).data("tag");
            $(".leftside").find('.filter-input:checked, .filter-input:selected').each(function () {
                if ($(this).data('tag') != uri) {
                    tags.push($(this).data('tag'))
                }
            });
            study_abroad = "False"
            if (study_abroad == "True") {
                tags.push("study_abroad");
                }
                paralellAjaxs(tags);
            }
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $('.filterBtn, .sortBtn').click(function () {
                $('#filtersModal').slideDown();
                $('body').addClass('overflowHide');
            });

            var hashed_url=window.location.hash
             if (hashed_url != '') {
                var is_filter = hashed_url.split('#')[1]
                if (is_filter){
                $('.filterBtn').trigger('click')
                }
             }

            if ($(window).width() <= 768) {
                $('#filtersModalBody .sidebar > div').first('.filter-list-container').addClass('selected');
                $(document).on("touchstart click", "#filtersModal .filter-list-container .filter-option", function () {
                    $(".filter-list-container").removeClass("selected"), $(this).parent().addClass("selected"), $(".filter-deta-outer").hide(), $(this).parent().find(".filter-deta-outer").show()
                });
            } else {
                $(document).on('click',".filter-list-container .filter-option",function () {
                    $(this).toggleClass("filterClose");
                    $(this).siblings().slideToggle();
                });
            }
            $('#filtersModal .close,#submit_filters').on("touchstart click", function () {
                $('#filtersModal').slideUp();
                $('body').removeClass('overflowHide');
            });

            loadSponseredListing();
        });

        $(document).on('click', '.remove_class', function () {
            removeFilter($(this))
        })


        $(document).on('click', '.btn-reset', function() {
            reLoadFilters($(this))
        })

        $(document).on('click', '.submitBtn', function(){
            $('#filtersModal').slideUp();

        })

        $(document).on('click', '.back-ic', function(){
            $('#filtersModal').slideUp();
            $('body').removeClass('overflowHide');
        })

        function callvirtualfilter(that)
        {
            $(that).parent('label').toggleClass('selected');
            var tag = $(that).data('tag')
            $(".leftside [data-tag='" + tag + "']").trigger('click');


        }


    function loadSponseredListing()
    {
        var tags = [];
        
            tags.push("india")
        

        study_abroad = "False"
        if (study_abroad == "True") {
            tags.push("study_abroad");
        }

        url = "/get_sponsored_listing/"
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: url,
            traditional: true,
            data: {
                'tags': tags,
                'stream_id': 'None',
                'level_id': "None",
                "sponsored_listing": 1,
                "url_name": "listings_index"
            }
        }).done(function (response) {
            if(response){
                $(".first-box").html( response);
            }

        });
    }

     try
      {
       let observer = new IntersectionObserver(dfpCallback, {root: null,rootMargin: '0px',threshold: .5});  
       let target = document.querySelector('.dfp');
       observer.observe(target);
      }
      catch(exc)
      {
         console.log(exc);
      }
}

var dfpCallback = (entries, observer) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) 
        {
            observer.unobserve(entry.target);
            requestIdleCallback(function(){
            var loadSecurePubAd = loadScript("https://securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js",'gpt-js');
        });

       }
      });
};
